#general

## login
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/login" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/login");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST login`


<!-- END_ba35aa39474cb98cfb31829e70eb8b74 -->

<!-- START_6858d18a63ce6267c99e7a7939a2d1b3 -->
## This is the short description

This can be an optional longer description of your API call, used within the documentation.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/afiliado/crear" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/crear");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST afiliado/crear`


<!-- END_6858d18a63ce6267c99e7a7939a2d1b3 -->

<!-- START_d3393c0db950f85a667de70ae0dcb693 -->
## afiliado/all
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/afiliado/all" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/all");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`GET afiliado/all`


<!-- END_d3393c0db950f85a667de70ae0dcb693 -->

<!-- START_466329454684d454600cc8aaacaa9229 -->
## afiliado/editar/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X PUT "http://localhost/afiliado/editar/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/editar/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST afiliado/delete`


<!-- END_028f20c1581a0286ff67967540acdc1f -->

<!-- START_25bd5914baedca0380e1cb60ee156f67 -->
## afiliado/comprar
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/afiliado/comprar" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/comprar");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST afiliado/comprar`


<!-- END_25bd5914baedca0380e1cb60ee156f67 -->

<!-- START_2b278f412dd290097076abf5eb47c8d2 -->
## afiliado/cuentaCorriente/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/afiliado/cuentaCorriente/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/cuentaCorriente/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`GET afiliado/cuentaCorriente/{id}`


<!-- END_2b278f412dd290097076abf5eb47c8d2 -->

<!-- START_05d8652aec7fafe223948fabe0c5cf16 -->
## afiliado/cuentaCorrienteAfiliados
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/afiliado/cuentaCorrienteAfiliados" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/afiliado/cuentaCorrienteAfiliados");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

## farmacia/crear
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/farmacia/crear" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/farmacia/crear");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`GET farmacia/all`


<!-- END_bb674c18811e9979135eb1496c9d358a -->

<!-- START_05b633539fefa10654bcf009099394d7 -->
## farmacia/editar/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X PUT "http://localhost/farmacia/editar/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/farmacia/editar/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`PUT farmacia/editar/{id}`


<!-- END_05b633539fefa10654bcf009099394d7 -->

<!-- START_32d26cb213419dc0c016f362a67632ef -->
## farmacia/find/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/farmacia/find/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/farmacia/find/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

## farmacia/delete
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/farmacia/delete" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/farmacia/delete");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST producto/crear`


<!-- END_283c5cdc338c27f85dc2a0eaba948692 -->

<!-- START_232694f329961ec9df5e203481729b9c -->
## producto/all
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/producto/all" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/producto/all");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`GET producto/all`


<!-- END_232694f329961ec9df5e203481729b9c -->

<!-- START_6876dab2d5447c5f73ad8f1828700dc1 -->
## producto/editar/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X PUT "http://localhost/producto/editar/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/producto/editar/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`PUT producto/editar/{id}`


<!-- END_6876dab2d5447c5f73ad8f1828700dc1 -->

<!-- START_52ddb9e0e185258f1e1c75634fd25e6d -->
## producto/find/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/producto/find/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/producto/find/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

## producto/delete
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://localhost/producto/delete" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/producto/delete");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`POST red/crear`


<!-- END_6a2970cad5d32d275ecd6d4d40315e67 -->

<!-- START_fdec25368286580ad562adb9456f41b5 -->
## red/all
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET -G "http://localhost/red/all" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/red/all");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

### HTTP Request
`GET red/all`


<!-- END_fdec25368286580ad562adb9456f41b5 -->

<!-- START_b71982c80139cf8143f2dd4057f57c9f -->
## red/editar/{id}
> Example request:

```bash
curl -X PUT "http://localhost/red/editar/{id}" 
```

```javascript
const url = new URL("http://localhost/red/editar/{id}");

let headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers: headers,
})
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(json => console.log(json));
```

```bash

```

```javascript

    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",

    headers: headers,
```
